Part - a (SQL Scripts)

**The scripts below are not complete. We have a large data base and the file size went to >22 MB when we included all the scripts which is not allowed on moodle. So, this file contains some scripts for all the tables.


drop table if exists administrator;
CREATE TABLE administrator (username varchar(25) primary key, password varchar(25) not null, name varchar(50) not null, address varchar(200), emailid varchar(150) not null CHECK (emailid ~* '^[A-Za-z0-9._%-]+@[A-Za-z0-9.-]+[.][A-Za-z]+$'), role varchar(30) not null check (role = 'Manager' or role='Employee'));

drop table if exists customer;
CREATE TABLE customer (username varchar(25) primary key, password varchar(25) not null, name varchar(50) not null, address varchar(200), emailid varchar(150) not null CHECK (emailid ~* '^[A-Za-z0-9._%-]+@[A-Za-z0-9.-]+[.][A-Za-z]+$'));
insert into customer values('mridul', 'mridul', 'mridul garg', 'kota', 'gmridul09@gmail.com');

drop table if exists cities;
CREATE TABLE cities (cityid serial primary key, countryname varchar(40) references countries(countryname), statename varchar(25), cityname varchar(25) NOT NULL, pincode bigint NOT NULL, stdcode bigint NOT NULL);

CREATE TABLE history (username varchar(25) references customer(username), planid integer references plan(planid), dateoftravel date, placeid integer unique not null, primary key (username, planid, dateoftravel));

CREATE TABLE schedule (username varchar(25) references customer(username), timeofevent timestamp not null, event varchar(100) not null, primary key (username, timeofevent));

CREATE TABLE spotrating (username varchar(25) references customer(username), cityid integer references cities(cityid), spotname varchar(100) not null, srating integer default 0 );

CREATE TABLE hotelrating (username varchar(25) references customer(username), cityid integer references cities(cityid), hotelname varchar(100) not null, hrating integer default 0);

CREATE TABLE tovisit (username varchar(25) references customer(username), planid integer references plan(planid), cityid integer references cities(cityid), spotname varchar(100) not null, dateoftravel date not null); 

CREATE TABLE friends (planid integer references plan(planid), friend varchar(25) references customer(username));

CREATE TABLE notification(planid integer references plan(planid), sender varchar(25) references customer(username), reciever varchar(25) references customer(username), seen boolean default 'f'); 

drop table if exists plan;
create table plan (planid serial primary key, planname varchar(50) NOT NULL);
insert into plan(planname) values('plan1');
insert into plan(planname) values('plan2');

insert into plan(planname) values('plan10');

create table wishList(username varchar(25) references customer(username), cityid integer references cities(cityid), spotname varchar(100));

PART - b (Queries)

This is for the description and rating of the spot on which the user has cilcked:

select description,rating from touristspots where cityid = ‘city-name’ and spotname =  
‘spot-name’;



This query is used to provide information about a hotel in particular city :

select * from hotel where cityid = ‘city-id’ and hotelname = ‘hotel-name’;



This Query is for providing information about the user :

select * from customer where username = ‘user-name’;



These set of queries are for the Current Plans . Where we provide information about the currently selected plan :

R1 = select * from tovisit where username = ‘user’ and planname = ‘plan’;
select c.name from customer as c,friend as f where f.planid IN (R1) and c.username 
= f.friend;



This Query provides information about history of the user:

select placeid from history where username = ‘user’ and dateoftravel = ‘date’ ;



These set of queries are for creating a new plan:

insert into plan (planname) values (‘name of plan’);
planid = select max(planid) from plan where planname = ’name of plan’ order by 
planid;
cityid = select cityid from cities where countryname = ‘country’ and statename = 
’statename’ and cityname = ‘cityname’;  
insert into tovisit values (‘username’, planid, cityid, ’spotname’, ‘dateoftravel’);
 


These set of queries are for adding to the wish list :

select cityid, cityname, statename, countryname from cities where cityid in (select 
cityid from touristspots where spotname = ‘spot’;);
cityid = select cityid from cities where cityname = city and statename = state and 
countryname = country;
insert into wishlist values (user, cityid, spot);


Query for searching a Spot:

By Spotname --
select * from touristspots where spotname = ‘spot’;

By Country --
select statename from states where countryname = ‘country’;

By State --
select cityname from cities where countryname = ‘country’ and statename = ‘state’;

By City --
R1 = select cityid from cities where countryname = ‘country’ and statename = ‘state’ 
and cityname = ‘city’;
select spotname from touristspots where cityid = R1 ;

Query executed at time of login Login:
select password from customer where username = ‘user’;
 

Queries for Editing Profile:

update customer set name = ‘newname’ where username = ‘user’;
update customer set password = ‘newpass’ where username = ‘user’;
update customer set  emailid = ‘newname’ where username = ‘user’;
update customer set  address = ‘newaddress’ where username = ‘user’;

Query for Sign Up:
insert into customer values (user, pass, name, address, emailid);
